# Thread: GATE Program during the 90s
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-program-during-the-90s.31937/>
**Subforum:** Dive Deeper with Dr. Kruse’s Exclusive Webinar!
**Posts:** 13
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### KFDags — 2025-11-25T21:08:37+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-program-during-the-90s.31937/post-363178>

It’s been a few months now since I first saw some videos out there (first on X) regarding the 90s Gifted and Talented Education (GATE) program and its alleged CIA involvement with mind control, remote viewing/psychic abilities, and even recruiting future agents. Some have compared it to the Stargate Project, which was a real operation. Not sure if anyone is familiar with what I’m rambling on about; I know another member brought this up in the forum months ago. He was from the same area as me, Rhode Island, although this program took place all over the US and a few in some other countries. Well, all I can say is I’m utterly weirded out. Why are all these former GATE students appearing to be coming out now, at the same time? I believe in coincidences less and less, the older I get.

My first instinct is to distrust whatever it is being blasted out there on the internet, but I can’t ignore the staggering number of similarities between these so-called GATE participants and me. Like many others in this program back in the 90s, they took me and some other students out of class (I was probably ~11 years old.) We were given the hearing tests with the giant headphones in a secluded room. If you heard a sound, you’d raise a hand or point to the corresponding ear. (i.e., raise your left hand if you hear a sound in the left ear, and do the opposite for the right side.) I also had some test done at the school that they claimed was to check for scoliosis. Up until recently I had assumed that everyone had these tests done in school, right? I do recall the pink liquid in cups (was told it’s a fluoride rinse,) the pink chewable tablets (was told it’s to highlight dental plaque) but I can’t remember if I actually used any of them.

However it started, I found myself in the Crusaders (or Crusades) Club. My mom remembers me being in this club but never knowing why. Once a week, I was pulled out of class to go be in this window-less room inside the school, along with some others. There were college-age students there helping us, mostly girls; they always dressed in light-colored but neutral clothing, oversized sweatshirts, matching sweatpants. One girl looked to me like Alanis Morissette; when I told her that, she got kind of offended. That’s the timeframe for when this was happening: I had my Jagged Little Pill cassette tape and cassette player with me for the bus ride so 1996 maybe.

Each new time we arrived to this club, there was a table with one or two piles of printed-out papers with puzzles or some type of word problem to solve. The papers were always just there to take, but we never had a teacher or any instruction. At first, no one made me do the work so I went with it, of course. (Duh.) But I began to get the sense that there was a reason that the work was there. Again, no one ever said we had to do this work. I started participating eventually. We also never got graded or any results.

Other than that, we just did fun activities to pass the time: watched movies, hung out, ate junk food, etc. For some reason, the only movie I remember we watched was The Ugly Dachshund, from 1966. The Crusades Club had no instructor or instructions and there was never any direction; it was unlike any other class I’ve had before or after.

I’ll post more to this strangeness when I get some more time. Just wanted to put it down here since maybe someone else has some substance to offer or maybe their own experience. Anytime I bring these subjects up with my family, all I get in reply is, “Oh,” or “I don’t remember.”

### KFDags — 2025-12-05T20:54:24+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-program-during-the-90s.31937/post-363615>

Over Thanksgiving, I asked my parents (they’re divorced) if they recalled the Crusades program I was in. My dad actually did: he recalled my mom being very excited over me being offered a spot in some special “enrichment program” for high IQ/high abilty children. He described the program as some type of additional education or special educational opportunities, separate from my regular classes.

When speaking with my mom, she remembered almost nothing (naturally.) She did say that my uncle suggested that I transfer to some school, in the City of Providence, that had a special giftedness program. That obviously never happened.

As an aside, this tiny detail (that I was, in fact, a gifted/high-ability child) is something that was kept from me until now, at nearly 40 years old. My parents’ obliviousness has been a lifelong frustration for me. I do love them, but I’m now having an identity crisis and re-thinking my entire existence on this random December afternoon.

### KFDags — 2025-12-05T23:29:49+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-program-during-the-90s.31937/post-363622>

> [S Hudson said:](/goto/post?id=363620)

Yes! They sound creepy as hell! Does the futuristic beeping bother anyone else on a visceral level or???

### doctorwu85 — 2025-12-08T03:09:40+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-program-during-the-90s.31937/post-363680>

That was me: [https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads...grams-an-offshoot-of-mkultra-and-darpa.30998/](https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-90s-public-school-gifted-programs-an-offshoot-of-mkultra-and-darpa.30998/)

And yeah, we grew up in the same state and we're the same age. Similar experience for me. Our room had windows and the activities didn't seem quite as sinister, but definitely followed the same pattern that many other people reported. I listed some specifics on that previous thread.

I'm 100% convinced it was a 3 letter agency-sponsored screening program for kids with 1) high intelligence/creativity that could benefit government agencies in the future, and/or b) certain types of parapsychological abilities

### HLG2025 — 2025-12-17T12:48:29+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-program-during-the-90s.31937/post-363987>

I was also in the “gifted program” from (asked/tested to be in it in 1st grade) 2nd grade onwards. This was in Miami, Florida. For me, it was the entirety of my class was a gifted class so i wasnt pulled out of normal class for a certain period of time to go into a special program, it was just i was totally in a gifted class for the base of my schooling, In middle school and high school electives were mostly not gifted so put with the normies and also AP classes were mixed with normies as well (so like kids who were in “honors” classes would go into AP classes sometimes). I graduated 44 out of 844 in my class with minimal effort. I dont recall anything strange or weird although i kind of wish i did because that woukd be a little more exciting…but i do agree that suddenly im hearing about this (im also almost 40) when i hadn’t seen or heard anything about it my entire life!! (i also relate to my parents obliviousness being a lifelong frustration, as my mom also remembers nothing)

### KFDags — 2026-02-09T21:26:38+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-program-during-the-90s.31937/post-366604>

Epstein seemed to have an interest in this so-called ‘pseudoscience.’

### [Age Verification | United States Department of Justice](https://www.justice.gov/epstein/files/DataSet%2011/EFTA02509560.pdf)

 www.justice.gov

### KFDags — 2026-02-09T21:49:50+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-program-during-the-90s.31937/post-366606>

For those unaware, this is the list of very common characteristics we former GATE students apparently share. No one checks off everything from this list, but most can say yes to the majority. Can’t speak for others here, but I have exactly zero in common with most other humans, mostly by choice. So finding all these former GATE students with the exact same qualities and experiences is disturbing.

### KFDags — 2026-02-10T23:07:12+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-program-during-the-90s.31937/post-366654>

At the same time the GATE classes started, mid-90s, my elementary school got its first DARE officer, Officer Currier. I thought it was great: he interrupted our mundane class, once a week, for an hour or so; we listened to 90s grunge, which I was all about; he talked about having positive self-esteem, avoiding drugs, not joining gangs, the whole thing. I tuned out all the fluff; no need to repeat the obvious.

Before he ended each DARE class, he’d do animal trivia. No one else in class knew jack shit about wildlife, so I won all the prizes, nearly every class. Also provided my guidance when he had trouble pronouncing the hard words. He stared confused when I explained that I wanted to be a herpetologist someday. He also learned the definition of herpetologist.

Officer Currier (now a school resource officer, no longer doing DARE) then showed up to my middle school, once I transferred there. I didn’t see him as much or as predictably as before, but he was always within reach, it felt. I thought it was comforting? He’d never fail to greet me by stating my full first and last name out loud.

Once, Officer Currier took me to his office; he showed me that a classmate had called me some nasty names, then posted it online. Just dumb teenager BS, back even before MySpace existed; nothing even remotely serious. Still never figured out how he found that post. Don’t know what happened to my classmate, but Officer Currier was pissed; way more than I was.

Then, 1999/2000, he followed me to my high school. I mentioned in my optimal journal how I used to skip school, almost constantly, to sleep. Well, had it not been for Officer Currier, I never would have gotten away with it! For 3 straight years. He knew my car and license plate so the rest was history.

At 17, I began my first serious relationship with my boyfriend. He was staying with mutual friends of ours, during this time, around 2003. I had never been to this friend’s house before. Guess who lived directly across the street from my boyfriend? None other than Officer Currier!

I never saw or heard from him again, though. By this time, I was working at a local pet store. That is exactly when my creepy stalker customer first appeared. His occupation? Law enforcement. Stay tuned!

### KFDags — 2026-02-11T19:35:18+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-program-during-the-90s.31937/post-366703>

Here’s the man himself, Officer Currier. The second picture is from the high school yearbook. Hey, if I’m on a list, may as well have fun with it, right?

### JenniferM — 2026-02-11T21:43:04+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-program-during-the-90s.31937/post-366717>

Wow! This is such a creepy story. Right up there with serial killers/stalkers.

### KFDags — 2026-02-13T00:11:31+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/gate-program-during-the-90s.31937/post-366782>

> [JenniferM said:](/goto/post?id=366717)
>
> Wow! This is such a creepy story. Right up there with serial killers/stalkers.

The thing is, he was always very kind & respectful to me. I never imagined something nefarious. And before I go any further, I will acknowledge that the bitter irony is not lost on me: my husband is a police officer. I am so deeply entrenched in whatever this thing is, it’s not even funny. How many lifelong coincidences equal a true living nightmare?

Anyway, the pet store was different. This super tall, muscular guy named Chris used to visit often, just to hang out; this started before I was hired. He was a cop, maybe early to mid-30s, married, and had twin baby girls. Total scumbag. Was previously lurking around my two female coworkers (including the owner’s sister), but then I became the favorite. He was extremely handsy, to put it lightly. I repeatedly complained to my boss to not leave me alone with him, but he did nothing. Never bothered to protect his own sister from him either, so no surprise there.

I quit and began working at a different pet store in another town. Figured I was all set. Then Chris started calling my cell phone and showing up at my new job. I’m still 17, by the way. I never gave him my info and couldn’t fathom how this happened. No need to ask because he explained that he took some belongings off my former boss’ desk, which contained my information.

I can’t remember what my parents said or did about this, if anything at all; and my boyfriend was too busy constantly celebrating being 21 years old, back then. So he kept showing up for a while, without any regard for the other customers there; he’d be there lurking. I didn’t know what to do. But abruptly, he disappeared one day. Stopped showing up, never called again, and that was it.

### flavin0 — 2026-02-16T05:17:23+0200

I got put in a gifted youth program at Stanford for a summer, though it wasn't called GATE. I just took a college class with some interesting people, living on campus for the summer. Maybe it was a cover.

I believe one of my favorite YouTubers named Jay Dyer got put in the GATE program as well. His work is great.

All the tests you mentioned in the beginning were done to all or most children. I remember them from the 70s.

I was never in the “gifted” program. My mom told us that me and all my siblings could have been in it because of very high IQs but my parents would not allow it. My Dad knew there was something off about it.

I don’t know much else except it seemed like a cool thing.

I was always wondering why my 3 older siblings all got to be on the “safety patrol” and I didn’t. My IQ was in the same range, high 130s, but I was not chosen for safety patrol. I got good grades.

Now I realize that’s it’s because I’m on the spectrum. They didn’t call it that then. And girls were ignored because the symptoms present differently. But I took a bunch of online tests because of the overlap with autism and Lyme disease. Now I realize it’s mitochondrial damage at the root cause.

Interesting to find out that you weren t being taught anything special.

Glad my Dad was a genius and knew.

# Thread: Russell Brand shoutout to Dr Jack
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/russell-brand-shoutout-to-dr-jack.31940/>
**Subforum:** The Cave
**Posts:** 1

### digitald3 — 2025-11-27T20:55:04+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/doctors-don%E2%80%99t-make-you-healthy.31947/post-363288>

Talked to a friend this am and he shared a story about a friend of his. That friend has stage 4 prostate cancer Went to a few centralized docs and got the same answer. Surgery, chemo and radiation. He decided to go the holistic centralized route. Went to a clinic in Mexico.a doc in Tennessee. Has spent about $200k on supplements and hyperbaric oxygen therapies and who knows what else. Loads of peptides and he can hardly keep track of he supplements. Apparently the tumors are smaller and he’s hoping for a few good years. He’s only 57.

When [@Jack Kruse](https://forum.jackkruse.com/members/1031/) says read the blogs. He means read them. This guy could have taken the $200k and moved to the tropics and started to heal. Stage 4 cancer is not the time to wake up. So it’s a crap shoot but if you learn the biophysics it makes sense that one can’t heal in the environment they got sick in.

Sometimes I understand why doctors don't break themselves out of the mould. What I've noticed in the UK is how much of a gatekeeper the medical regulator (GMC) is. I used to be involved in regulatory work, and I saw how my own regulator (dental) acted in a way that was against the best interests of UK dentists. A lot of that was down to the ego of the expert witnesses used and the "blue on blue" complaints by dentists against other dentists.

Through COVID, I know of 3 doctors who were struck off the medical register for going against the dogma of the vaccine. Jacks favourite (lol) **Dr. Aseem Malhotra** was almost struck off after complaints were made against him... not by patients but by younger dentists who didn't have his experience or his training. It was also hospital management crushing any kind of counter to the narrative they wanted to push.

Presently there are 2 doctors I've heard of who are suspended due to their anti-zionist views.
So yeah, having principles and a commitment to the truth comes at a cost

You have rampant caries - here is what you need to do so you aren't paying for my next car
You have perio - Learn these skills and avoid X/Y/Z so you keep your teeth
You have dental anxiety - Here are the resources you can use to fix that
etc etc

### digitald3 — 2025-11-30T01:15:49+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/doctors-don%E2%80%99t-make-you-healthy.31947/post-363370>

> [PIAZ said:](/goto/post?id=363367)
>
> Aside from the obvious (non-native EMF, sun, sleep..) is there another direction for TMJ? Please let me know, I'm told I have it.

Everyone has a TMJ, TMJ is short of the Temporal Mandibular Joint.. or the joint that connects the lower jaw, ie the Mandible, to the skull or more specifically the temporal bone in the head.. So everyone with a lower jaw has a TMJ

Now some have TMJ dysfunction which is a broad catch all diagnosis for a few types of issues.. the two most common are:
Related to pain in the muscles that make the TMJ complex work.. these muscles are all connected to head and neck region and TMJ pain can radiate in many areas from just the muscles alone.. if you've ever heard of people having botox injected for their TMJ, this is what its doing. its paralyzing the muscles. there are other kinder ways to calm muscles down, but the sun is the best IMHO

The TMJ also has a piece of cartilage that separates the lower jaw and the head.. this is called the TMJ disk. this disk can get damaged and displaced.. this is most likely the cause of TMJ's that pop and or click.. if the disk is badly damaged this can lead to a bone on bone condition and can lead to loss of bone at the joint level and this can alter the way the teeth come together. this can also be related to osteoarthritis in the TMJ joint. There are surgical options for a displaced disk, sadly the research isn't very positive on that approach.. if the joint has lost enough bone there are joint replacements that are becoming more common... again, imho Dr. Jacks rx is most likely the best alternative

Usually if the joint isn't painful but has some joint sounds I will usually monitor for bony changes at the joint level as this can be a sign of arthritis or changes in the way the teeth come together..

if you don't have symptoms that affect the way you live, then yes in my view the circadian rx or Dr Jacks rx is the best one can do... work to rebuild Beckers current of regeneration... obviously if you are having pain or dysfunction it might make sense to find a clinician you trust to get a solid diagnosis of what the condition of the TMJ is and that may alter the rx for you.. things like bite splints can be used temporarily to alleviate initial symptoms while working on the light story... Most TMJ dysfunction is a light story.. fix the light fix the problem..

### Anthony Smith — 2025-12-06T09:12:20+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/anywhere-with-no-trails-in-the-sky.31967/post-363627>

**Chemtrails are real** - BUT - not every trail lingering in the sky is a Chemtrail.
Atmospheric conditions (temperature, humidity etc) and altitude dictate how long a CONTRAIL lingers behind a plane.
CONTRAILS can cross the whole sky and stay as cloud in the upper atmosphere for a long time.

Be concerned and complain about REAL things . . .
if we complain about natural phenomena (out of ignorance) we loose any voice (credibility) we MAY of had to fight the real fight(s).

### Anthony Smith — 2025-12-06T21:45:07+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/anywhere-with-no-trails-in-the-sky.31967/post-363643>

Like I said CHEMTRAILS (weather modifications) are real - BUT . . .
Are you on a flight path? There are 10’s of thousands of commercial flights every day.
Plane goes over. Altitude + weather conditions allow the trail to linger. The trail drifts, the next plane flys over etc. All of a sudden the sky is covered.
Do you see more in the winter than the summer or vica-versa? Morning vs afternoon? Is it a high or low pressure day where you live?

My wife never payed much attention to the sky/clouds. All of a sudden she stated looking up (with all the talk of chemtrails etc) and was amazed at all the different cloud formations at different times. That is so unusual she would say about a VERY normal formation - that she had never noticed before. We live under the main north/south flight path on the west coast. Some days lots of flights bit no contrails, other days (different weather) lines all over the sky. I was a professional photographer, a natural sky is important in photos, I pay attention. Lingering contrails happen . . . and so do chemtrails.

If you are no way near a flight path and you see “trails” criss crossing the sky, good chance they are spraying.

# Thread: Help needed re: mitigating buried electrical cable issues in a coastal area with a high water table
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/help-needed-re-mitigating-buried-electrical-cable-issues-in-a-coastal-area-with-a-high-water-table.31984/>
**Subforum:** Feedback/Suggestions
**Posts:** 6
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Wilma Without a W — 2025-12-07T00:02:59+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/help-needed-re-mitigating-buried-electrical-cable-issues-in-a-coastal-area-with-a-high-water-table.31984/post-363647>

Hi, peeps.

Got a bit of a dilemma in a house I'm rehabbing in the costa del Sol area of El Salvador, which is located in a condo/development which is right on the beach, which means that the water table is fairly high, especially during the rainy season.

The electrician had what I thought was a great idea in that he moved the electric meter from the wall of the house to a location on a perimeter wall which is right on the driveway, far from the house.

Unfortunately, that meant that he had to bury the cables going from the meter to the house along said perimeter wall. The cables are encased in orange PVC piping which is rated for ground contact and they're buried maybe a foot and a half down.

There are at least three ground rods which follow the same route maybe 2 m apart starting from the wall of the house towards where the meter is.

I okayed this thinking that it was preferable to having a rat's nest of cables right above my head.

But now I'm doing research specific to this area and what I'm reading is to bury the cable about 2 m down, which is going to definitely hit the water table here.

And in my limited understanding hitting the water table isn't so much an issue for the cables themselves because that orange PVC pipe is rated for ground contact, but that the water or moisture in the ground can actually amplify the range that the nnEMF travel.

The electrician is coming tomorrow and so I have to tell him what I want done because I don't think the way it is currently is going to be okay from an nnemf perspective.

Does anyone have any educated thoughts on the issue?

I suppose once he connects the cables to the meter and the other end into the breaker box I'll be able to take some readings and have a better idea of what's going on.

The unfortunate bit is that once he connects the cables it'll be a lot more work to disconnect everything to bury it lower.

Thanks in advance for any thoughts on the matter.

### Mat.I — 2025-12-08T07:40:34+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/help-needed-re-mitigating-buried-electrical-cable-issues-in-a-coastal-area-with-a-high-water-table.31984/post-363683>

> [Wilma Without a W said:](/goto/post?id=363647)
>
> Does anyone have any educated thoughts on the issue?

Not enough technical info here to add meaningful feedback.. What type of underground cable.is proposed? Service current rating? Your original readings? Single or 3 phase? What is the purpose of the 3 x ground rods ?

### Mat.I — 2025-12-08T07:45:54+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/help-needed-re-mitigating-buried-electrical-cable-issues-in-a-coastal-area-with-a-high-water-table.31984/post-363684>

> [Mat.I said:](/goto/post?id=363683)
>
> Not enough technical info here to add meaningful feedback.. What type of underground cable.is proposed? Service current rating? Your original readings? Single or 3 phase? What is the purpose of the 3 x ground rods ?

Also did any one check for service side Neutral issues and imbalances? E.g. what are your N vs A clamp meter loads?? Was neutral to ground current t checked? Plus N.to E volts.. I wouldn't be making any substantial changes until this basic level is checked...

### Wilma Without a W — 2025-12-08T21:09:28+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/help-needed-re-mitigating-buried-electrical-cable-issues-in-a-coastal-area-with-a-high-water-table.31984/post-363703>

Hi, Mat. Thanks for your reply. I'm going to need to ask the electrician the why of the three ground rods. I didn't have the house formally checked out from an nnemf perspective when I purchased it, and I'm in the process of trying to set up a proper evaluation now, before I go any further. # Thread: Palpitations advice
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/palpitations-advice.31985/>
**Subforum:** Optimal Fitness
**Posts:** 5
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### S Hudson — 2025-12-07T00:57:44+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/palpitations-advice.31985/post-363651>

Around this time of year I have a tendency to get palpitations of varying severity (been that way for about 4 years). After seeing the cardiologist for a full cardiac screen 2 years back, he diagnosed it as Vagal nerve agitation due to sinus irritation from fungal spores caused by the increased moisture (I live in a very wooded area). Apparently, according to him at least, its a common presentation for a 53 year old male at this time of year.
Last year it was barely noticeable.

This is the only year I've done any meaningful sun exposure, and I've been hitting every sunrise. There was a period at the beginning of the year, but, surprise surprise, most of spring and summer was palpitations free.

This November, its come on like a freight train which I find strangely ironic.
I had booked several weeks away in the sun, to return just before xmas, but I really don't feel safe flying with the symptoms experienced this week and have cancelled my trip away with the hope that I can be away for most of winter post new year.

I live in 5g dead zone with even limited 4g, I sleep with the electricity off and have no wifi and have meter tested my sleep sanctuary. The palpitations seem to be better with light exercise, and although my heart rate is elevated at rest, it's not by much. I know I need to get into the sun, but I'll admit that fear of falling ill abroad and the discomfort of this is stopping me. Or is this my mind just putting road blocks up to stop me making the required change? Wouldn't surprise me.

It can be a horrible symptom, that almost feeds itself.

I suspect that there is an anxiety aspect to this, with the two conditions feeding on each other.
Jack, would you still recommend the cold therapy for someone with this presentation, or do you have insufficient info to make that call?

Thanks
SH

### Mat.I — 2025-12-17T07:01:54+0200

[@Anthony Smith](https://forum.jackkruse.com/members/26765/) - I have nothing absolute concrete on this other than apply first principles. I agree re: the microwave effects.. However, think about how induction operates, it using rapidly oscillating mag fields (tens of khz) to induce currents in the pan which heats / cooks the food by surface area contact etc.. If you are being super technical the resistance of the pan would convert these "eddy" currents into heat via joule heating. So looking at the basics of this poses the following question - what is cooking your food that you ingest? IMO you have gone too far downstream re: mag field > eddy currents > pan heats > IR + conduction (you are at the last 2). It is the final carrier but at the cost of delivering the mag fields. So directly (i.e. direct heating) in isolation is not what I consider as "bad" it is the indirect effects that your food is being "cooked" in a highly oscillating mag field.

Some will say this doesn't matter as once it hits your body it is processed and dealt with etc.. However, I do not think it is optimal as you are introducing all this artificial noise into your food as the main driver of the cooking process. I believe that the pathway to heat matters as there is "structure" and "information" in food. What will add more disorder heat alone or oscillating high frequency mag fields + heat? = more noise. Think about what impact this would have on foods water, proteins + lipids etc..

# Thread: Light, Water, Grounding and a crow

**Posts:** 2
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### JenniferM — 2025-12-13T22:27:28+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/light-water-grounding-and-a-crow.32007/post-363860>

We had a crow that started hanging around about 2 years ago. We became friends during that time. He would greet me in the mornings from his perch in a pine tree. Eventually he would accept pears and begin to talk to me in crow squawk. I would respond like I was talking to a baby, lol. The most awesome part of befriending Oscar the crow is when I discovered Dr. Kruse and began watching the sunrise and getting sun throughout the day. Oscar seemed to be pleased I was getting up earlier and spending more time outside. He is even more vocal in the early mornings now, like he is happier That I am out there for the sunrise. He watches me all the time. Today I was getting all the sun mother nature would give me. Oscar flew over to perch in a tree across from. While flying over he dropped a feather. I watched it fall. Got up and found the feather in the field, held it up to him and said Thank you. He flew away to do crow things I guess like he always does. It made me realize just how important that connection to all things nature is amazing when you least expect it. I love Oscar the crow and the feather is now my new bookmark. Thanks Dr. Kruse

Why should we eat MUFAS with DHA and not saturated fats?

Do saturated fats limit DHA absorption?

I am having a hard time finding corresponding information regarding this.

I love butter but almost all my meals have fish in it.

### Mat.I — 2025-12-20T04:43:50+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/why-mufas-with-dha-meals.32029/post-364063>

> [Tjmorki6 said:](/goto/post?id=364060)
>
> Just read EPI PALEO RX
> Great book, people need to read it, loved it.
>
> Why should we eat MUFAS with DHA and not saturated fats?
>
> Do saturated fats limit DHA absorption?
>
> I am having a hard time finding corresponding information regarding this.
>
> I love butter but almost all my meals have fish in it.

Due to the structure of DHA (6 double bonds). MUFAS keep the membranes fluid/flexible so the DHA can move / twist / bend and signal better etc.. Vs Sat fats they stiffen membranes and constrain the DHA (still absorbed) but signalling will be impacted etc..

### Adamo — 2025-12-27T15:21:32+0200

It seems obvious that a lot of history is a bold-face lie, with perhaps ~20% truth to it. There is evidence of previous "catastrophe(s)" and civilizations building things (and in ways) that should never have been possible given their supposed level of knowledge/technology/etc.

But there are too many people claiming to know exactly what and how and why and it really is speculation. Too many best guesses without the "smoking gun" kind of evidence.

As a "public" or "society," we do not have enough information to know exactly what happened. What we can discern is that a lot of what we are taught is non-sense. But these new theories coming out all of the time and gaining huge traction on the Internet do seem to have a big of "psy-op" or counter-op vibes to them... there is a lot of divide, sub-divide, subterfuge happening by means of the Internet. We have been in WWIII for quite some time now, and a big component of it is mental warfare.

There needs to be more hard evidence and data put together to support these theories rather than strong assumption and imagery. We are so far gone as a collective that it is not enough to ground us at this point. I do not say this because I am only scientific or left-brain minded, but we are so untethered from what is, as a collective, that we need to really be accurate in our approach to understanding wtf is really and has really gone on.

If you are really into these kinds of topics, but want more "solid" research, you can look into Archaix, Dark Journalist and the likes of Joseph P. Farrell. They cross this topic without a lot of the pre-conceived knowing of what we are looking at and with a more scholarly approach. They are not Tartaria-centric, but they cross these discussions points in their research that tie together a lot of the historical narratives.

# Thread: Home water treatment question -- Flow Tech Device?
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/home-water-treatment-question-flow-tech-device.32048/>
**Subforum:** The Cave
**Posts:** 1
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### ahermann91 — 2025-12-26T21:55:36+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/home-water-treatment-question-flow-tech-device.32048/post-364237>

We bought a new home and I've now had 3 plumbers, all from different service companies, separately recommend I install a FlowTech device that somehow descales my water lines and reduces biofilm / bacteria. The fact that all three of them came up with the recommendation (my house is 1912 build), made me feel less worried about being conned into a product that's a scam--I think it does actually work doing the things it says it does. But my brain went to associated health questions. It pulses the water (I think!?) with low frequency RF. Just don't know the implications / concerns / how water is affected/if this is a clear thing to avoid or if this somehow does improve the overall water quality.

# Thread: What water purifier do you use for showering?
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/what-water-purifier-do-you-use-for-showering.32088/>
**Subforum:** Beginners Area
**Posts:** 4
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### BrunoB — 2026-01-06T02:51:48+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/what-water-purifier-do-you-use-for-showering.32088/post-364815>

Hello, good day. I read that reverse osmosis is the best, but it can't be used for showering because it produces water very slowly. How can you purify water from heavy metals or other carcinogenic substances? Or do you have a giant reverse osmosis system for showering?
Thanks

### Adamo — 2026-01-06T03:17:23+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/what-water-purifier-do-you-use-for-showering.32088/post-364816>

An entire house system can soften the water (if needed) and has carbon filtration to remove the chlorine, chemicals, etc. in the water. No pressure issues at all.

Some will argue that the water from RO "has no life," but it is one of the most accessible/effective ways to purify your water from a city/municipal source.

### BrunoB — 2026-01-06T13:03:37+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/what-water-purifier-do-you-use-for-showering.32088/post-364846>

> [Adamo said:](/goto/post?id=364816)
>
> An entire house system can soften the water (if needed) and has carbon filtration to remove the chlorine, chemicals, etc. in the water. No pressure issues at all.
>
> Some will argue that the water from RO "has no life," but it is one of the most accessible/effective ways to purify your water from a city/municipal source.

What kind of whole-house water purification system do you use? What's it called?
Yes, unfortunately, that water isn't alive, but it's better to eliminate everything than to shower with "living" water containing cyanide, mercury, lead, and other filth that they blame on large-scale mining.

### Adamo — 2026-01-06T14:51:43+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/what-water-purifier-do-you-use-for-showering.32088/post-364849>

> [BrunoB said:](/goto/post?id=364846)
>
> What kind of whole-house water purification system do you use? What's it called?
> Yes, unfortunately, that water isn't alive, but it's better to eliminate everything than to shower with "living" water containing cyanide, mercury, lead, and other filth that they blame on large-scale mining.

I am not certain if there is a particular name. Companies try naming their systems to differentiate.

The water enters the dwelling from the street/city lines. From that, the water line goes into a 2-stage large canister/cylinder filtration system that has a softener bin attached where you put Sodium rocks in (softner salt).

Depending on your usage needs (how many people in the home), I have seen 1 cylinder, 2 cylinder and 4 cylinder systems.

Then you can have an additional counter-top or under-the-sink RO system and storage vessel for drinking/cooking water.

I hope that this helps.

══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Anna Dunn — 2026-01-08T02:33:34+0200

### jaedyn — 2026-01-08T05:02:49+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/daylight-tablet-recommendations.32103/post-364959>

> [Anna Dunn said:](/goto/post?id=364951)
>
> I’m recliner/bed bound so use iPad a lot. What’s a good daylight tablet to replace it? What’s a good laptop for my teen kids? One will start uni this yr, the other is at high school. This one was mentioned in the dec 2025 pow wow. [https://daylightcomputer.com](https://daylightcomputer.com). Is that the recommended one? If so, how do we access the discount and keyboard that was mentioned? I just joined btw and still learning.

Hi Anna,

Yes that is the daylight computer they would have spoken about in the PowWow, I haven't listened to it yet myself so unsure about the discount. Maybe Christy from support could help with that?

I don't believe there is a full-blown mito friendly laptop being made yet that I'm aware of (others on the forum may know something though). The daylight could be used for a lot of tasks and then only use the laptops when absolutely needed.

Try to use them whilst outside as much as possible, wifi and any other signal always off, hardwired internet connection with shielded cabling, never use whilst charging the laptop, always have the nightlight feature on (lowering blue light) or install a red film over the screen. I don't need to use laptops etc too often for work so I haven't deep dived into all the nitty gritty details but there's been a few discussions on the forum if you try the search function.

# Thread: Daylight Computer
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/daylight-computer.32107/>

### optimal2024 — 2026-01-08T21:01:20+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/daylight-computer.32107/post-364998>

Does anyone have a daylight computer? I wondered how people are getting on with it?
Also I asked them about their keyboard and mouse they offer and they replied saying it connect via bluetooth - is this not defeating the object of this computer?

### Mat.I — 2026-01-09T09:00:07+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/daylight-computer.32107/post-365031>

I personally just use a laptop / tablet that is hardwired and grounded outside with IRIS adjusted for viewing whilst in full sun.. I posted my desk setup somewhere in the forum..

### Szen — 2026-01-09T09:58:40+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/daylight-computer.32107/post-365032>

It can connect by bluetooth (can be disabled + airplane mode), but it also has x1 USB-C port below for wired.

If you want to use it more like a laptop(or more than 1 accessory) than a degoogled android tablet, you'll need a multiport adapter.

Also make sure you have your own wall plug or portable charger - only has USB-C to USB-C cable and a stylus out of the box.

Screen is legit really good on the eyes.

### DrSuzanneH7 — 2026-01-10T03:33:16+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/daylight-computer.32107/post-365078>

I have one and I really like it. I just load the files or blogs that I want to read onto it and read them at night without disturbing my sleep. So you can get on using Wi-Fi but then you just cut the Wi-Fi out and use it. You can also download books onto it and use it like a regular tablet using Wi-Fi. But I don't have Wi-Fi on so I just use it as a reader.

However recently it had some strange glitch and I couldn't get it to repair even with the factory reset. Customer service is very good and they are going to replace it.

# Thread: DIY spectrometer using a smartphone
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/diy-spectrometer-using-a-smartphone.32120/>
**Subforum:** The Cave
**Posts:** 3
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Daulatwant — 2026-01-12T16:24:31+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/diy-spectrometer-using-a-smartphone.32120/post-365205>

There is tutorials how to make basic spectrometers like this, I tried making one before with a webcam and it didn't produce very good results. But this time I tried using my phone instead as the camera. I downloaded iVCam software on pc and phone that lets you use phone as webcam over USB and it has good controls for the camera. Then I used Theremino Spectrometer software on Windows. And calibrated it using a CFL bulb, calibration needs to be redone every time cause this is a loose contraption, and moving things will mess up the calibration. A piece of CD is used to scatter the different wavelengths, I cut slots into a bottle cap to hold it and fixed it with a screw through the outside of the box into the bottle cap, I can twist the screw to change the CD angle. Lining everything up so the light hits the CD just right is tricky.

Please try again later.", "lightbox\_start\_slideshow": "Start slideshow", "lightbox\_stop\_slideshow": "Stop slideshow", "lightbox\_full\_screen": "Full screen", "lightbox\_thumbnails": "Thumbnails", "lightbox\_download": "Download", "lightbox\_share": "Share", "lightbox\_zoom": "Zoom", "lightbox\_new\_window": "New window", "lightbox\_toggle\_sidebar": "Toggle sidebar" } [](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/img_20260112_132453-jpg.33119/)[](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/img_20260112_132531-jpg.33120/)[](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/img_20260112_132411-jpg.33122/)[](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/img_20260112_125826-jpg.33118/)[](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/red-filter-incandescent-jpg.33133/)

### Daulatwant — 2026-01-12T16:39:09+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/diy-spectrometer-using-a-smartphone.32120/post-365206>

Here is the spectrum of a small dim incandescent, obviously that's not what the spectrum should look like, the red drops off because cameras have an infrared filter built in.

[](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/incandescent-jpg.33125/)[](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/img_20260112_125638-jpg.33131/)

But besides the relative brightness of each wavelength not being very accurate. I was surprised how sensitive it turned out being.

I bought some phosphor red led (blue diode converted to red) to test out, and it was able to pick up the blue light.

[](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/img_20251223_162121-jpg.33124/)

Here I measured a tiny very dim 660nm led and then a 590nm led and it was spot on.

[](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/spectrum-deep-red-jpg.33126/) [](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/asd-jpg.33127/)
This is more like what the previous red led should have looked like. The little, ripples along the bottom is just camera noise cause these measurements were very dim.

### Daulatwant — 2026-01-12T16:52:03+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/diy-spectrometer-using-a-smartphone.32120/post-365207>

This is my Samsung phone OLED screen with blue and green completely blocked by software.

[](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/untitled-jpg.33128/)

This is an old laptop LCD with F.LUX set to the lowest setting. At first glance it looks like it's doing something, this is what I meant saying it's surprisingly sensitive, again the rippling at along the bottom is just the noise floor of the camera at a high ISO level and you can still pick up on the small amount of blue light. But tilting the display reveals lots of blue and green leaking at an angle through the LCD. This as an old LCD, I don't know how an IPS LCD would compare.

[](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/lcd-jpg.33129/) .[](https://forum.jackkruse.com/attachments/lcd-from-an-angle-jpg.33130/)

Quite useful for testing LED lights.

I even laid naked about an hour when sun available and temperatures were mild for few days In the beginning,I felt great and had so much energy. However, starting 3 days ago , I started feeling totally awake when I get up at night ( I have an urological condition) and could not get back to sleep. I felt zero sleep pressure. ### Mr.AJ — 2026-01-13T20:17:40+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/no-sleep-pressure-after-getting-up-at-night.32128/post-365271>

There can be a case where during longer dark cycles it's normal to have a short wake up in the middle of the night and then fall back to sleep in 30 min to an hour.

But, it's probably the case that it's winter and light cycles are shorter/less intense which means you have less margin of safety after sunset. You live in Houston which means nnEMF and use of ALAN are likely the problem.

Test your environment. Only use candles after sunset. No screens. No LED's.

I'm telling you this from experience. Every time I try to use a screen post sunset even with IRIS on I get QE#47 bitch slapped.

edit: Probably need more sun time during the day also. = more melatonin production during the day.

### ToothDriller — 2026-01-13T21:15:27+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/no-sleep-pressure-after-getting-up-at-night.32128/post-365273>

So regarding your condition. Enlarged Prostate or frequency? I ask because if your are not staying in a proper sleep cycle your brain registers your bladder is full. Actually we never completely empty our bladders always some left. So if you are in a deep sleep say REM and you have a breathing issue that pulls you out and you wake up and say I gotta go. Its the breathing issue that created that signal
So my first thought is there more a sleep issue? Snoring, UARS, or sleep apnea. If so there are things I can suggest to help that are non-invasive.
Second I agree with AJ in that make sure your blue light is blocked at night.
More sun during the day means more melatonin as long as no sunglasses which based on your comments I doubt you wear them.
There are many factors so I would give it a few days and don't stress to much about it. Hit that sunset light to signal your body, minimize or eliminate food within a few hours of bedtime and make sure you block blue light.
Even lights from the street can signal the body to wake up so make sure nothing outside changed either.

Multiple theories on this:

-   **Illuminati Initiation Rituals:** the black eye is a physical mark of an initiation ritual into a secret society like the Illuminati. Believers suggest the bruise is a result of a physical "soul-scalping" or a painful rite of passage.
-   **Adrenochrome Withdrawal:** black eyes are sometimes linked to the "adrenochrome" theory. .
-   **Alien or Parasitic Possession:** More fringe theories suggest the bruise is the entry point for an reptilian entity that takes over the host's body. A big favourite with David Icke
-   **Vril Society & Clones:** the bruise marks the point where a biological "Vril" parasite enters the optic nerve to replace the individual with a clone or a mind-controlled puppet
-   **Human nature**: People can be really clumsy or have violent partners. Knowing how sociopathic most politicians and celebrities are...

so, take your pick lol

# Thread: New "NTP-LITE" Studies Fail to Replicate 2018 NTP Findings
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-ntp-lite-studies-fail-to-replicate-2018-ntp-findings.32206/>
**Subforum:** The EMF Rx
**Posts:** 5
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Guy Houri — 2026-01-29T13:23:50+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-ntp-lite-studies-fail-to-replicate-2018-ntp-findings.32206/post-366085>

Two new replication studies from Japan and South Korea (referred to as **NTP-LITE**) were recently published (Jan 2026), claiming no significant link between cell phone radiation and cancer. However, a deeper look at the data reveals several red flags:

-   **Low Statistical Power:** These studies used significantly fewer animals (only ~70 per group vs. hundreds in the original NTP), making it nearly impossible to prove "statistical significance" for rare tumors.
-   **High Background Illness:** In some cases, up to 20% of the animals (14 out of 70) developed tumors, but since the control groups (Sham) also had high rates of illness, researchers dismissed the findings as "within historical range."
-   **Methodological Gaps:** The studies only tested one modulation (CDMA) and one power level 4W/kg, ignoring the GSM modulation which showed the strongest cancer links in the original 2018 NTP study.

**Sources:**

-   **[**Israeli NoRad4U Blog**](https://www.norad4u.co.il/2026/01/29/11491/?fbclid=IwY2xjawPoHaBleHRuA2FlbQIxMQBzcnRjBmFwcF9pZBAyMjIwMzkxNzg4MjAwODkyAAEeWN8ZDCxd1K90MeoZjgFI1qNH_iBQjlQseYFRcrYb8LGVYYkz4htY1k312VA_aem_ix5R8wkZEXyymFfwafSvbg)**
-   [**Microwave News**](https://microwavenews.com/short-takes-archive/ntp-lite-korea)

**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-ntp-lite-studies-fail-to-replicate-2018-ntp-findings.32206/post-366091>

> [DLO said:](/goto/post?id=366599)

> I dont see any mito connection

Well, at first i got thrown for a tangent because the Mito Regiment was part of the Imperial Japanese Army's 14th Division, serving in the Second Sino-Japanese War before being deployed to the Pacific Theatre. The term Mito also references the Jinrai Butai kamikaze Special Attack Corp. And yet, none of your videos were related to the Japanese. So then I'm thinking, being where we are in this quantum forum, your use of the term **"Mito Soldiers"** referred to the health philosophy cantered on cellular energy, and you are thus using Native American soldiers as a symbolic or literal example of "peak" human biology.

Now let's look at my examples:

**Paddy Mayne**
He was an international rugby player and amateur boxer known for "Herculean" strength, such as allegedly ripping control panels out of aircraft with his bare hands. Mayne had a reputation for incredible night vision and the ability to navigate or "sense" the enemy in total darkness. He spent years living in the harsh desert and European wilderness.

**Carton De Weart**
He was shot in the face, head, stomach, ankle, leg, hip, and ear- suffering 11 injuries in all over numerous wars. When a doctor refused to amputate his shattered fingers in 1915, he reportedly bit them off himself. A person with poorly mitochondria would have died from infection or systemic inflammation after just one of those injuries. He survived two plane crashes, escaped a POW camp by tunnelling out at age 61 (staying on the run for 8 days), and survived a broken back later in life.
He had incredible cellular repair and stress tolerance

**Anders Lassen**
Like the Native American scouts, Lassen was an expert hunter from childhood who preferred the outdoors to school. During his training in the Scottish Highlands, Lassen reportedly stalked and killed a stag using only a commando knife.
Lassen had superior night vision and was famous for his night raids. His Victoria Cross citation describes him single-handedly destroying three machine-gun nests in total darkness and killing 8 enemy soldiers at Lake Comacchio, despite being mortally wounded.

If these 3 men didn't have optimised mitochondria, I don't know who has
All three possessed extreme physical endurance and sensory awareness, which can easily be attributed to high-functioning mitochondria

# Thread: A glossary of biochemical terms from Grok
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/a-glossary-of-biochemical-terms-from-grok.32237/>
**Subforum:** Beginners Area
**Posts:** 2
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### flavin0 — 2026-02-07T23:57:22+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/a-glossary-of-biochemical-terms-from-grok.32237/post-366507>

I was trying to read a paper titled Dynamics and Environment of Mitochondrial Water as Detected by 1H NMR, and I'm not really that keen on biochemical studies, so I asked Grok to make me a glossary of the biochemical terms used as well as provide an analogy of the relaxation with coupled oscillators which I am more familiar with. it's attached. It's a bit more than a glossary actually because Grok read the paper and the results of the paper are sprinkled in the glossary.

### flavin0 — 2026-02-08T04:59:57+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/a-glossary-of-biochemical-terms-from-grok.32237/post-366527>

Okay, I think I have an improved mechanistic mental model on what Dr. Kruse is really describing every time he mentions something about the mitochondria. I was inspired by the latest interview between Dr. Sara Pugh and Dr. Glen Jeffry.

The mitochondria can be approximated as a circuit with four complexes, connected not by the wires you'd imagine in an electrical circuit but by hydrogen bonding networks in the uniquely confined "nanowater" between complexes. Energy is defined in physics as the capacity for performing useful work. The useful work we get out of the mitochondria is the ability to live, breath, move, think, etc. and the complexes might be exploiting the motion of charge carriers between complexes to supply the resources to do the aforementioned useful work.

Recall from intro electromagnetism class that every conductive material such as a copper wire has an innate baseline resistance to the motion of charge carriers through it. This is sort of hand waved away a little bit in intro E&M but it is because the motion of charge carriers is somewhat messy (maybe turbulent in a nonliving system, but that may be a stretch considering turbulence is a term to denote fluid motion and classical electrodynamics shies away from characterizing simple circuits with fluid dynamics), and it takes the application of an electrical potential gradient to basically ensure a neat, macroscopic, classical vectorial direction of motion of charge carriers.

Anyways, the resistivity in a copper wire is analogous to the viscosity of the confined water molecules. Or, another way to put it is that the baseline relatively higher viscosity of the confined water over regular water molecules floating about in a bulk volume is like the baseline resistivity to the motion of charge carriers (jargon alert: via the "Grotthuss mechanism") of the mitochondria's nanowater hydrogen bonding network.

The analogy between coupled oscillators and the hydrogen bonding network is key: the water molecules are connected like a matrix of masses (atoms) connected by springs (bonds). From modern physics class we know infrared is going to act more wavelike than particle-like as a general rule of thumb. The spectral reason that sunlight is so much better than artificial lighting is that infrared acts as an external factor that improves the motion of charge carriers between complexes by altering the viscosity via a wave-like and not particle-like mechanism, probably affecting the modes of oscillation rather than direct particle collision type phenomena.

Obviously coupled oscillator problems get messy quickly, the most of them avoiding closed-form analytic solutions. And we are talking about a bunch of masses coupled by springs so this is as far as I can go mechanistically at this point. And also I still don't know much about the Grotthuss mechanism.

What do you guys think? Am I getting AI psychosis a bit or am I on the right track


══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# Thread: Quick Start Guide to El Salvador
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/quick-start-guide-to-el-salvador.32274/>
**Subforum:** Beginners Area
**Posts:** 1
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### beast — 2026-02-18T22:04:01+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/quick-start-guide-to-el-salvador.32274/post-367111>

I spent 6 weeks in El Salvador.
Here is everything you need to know to get set up there quickly.

This guide covers:
1\. Good Light
2\. Good Magnetism
3\. Healthy Food
4\. Language Barrier
5\. Transportation
6\. Emergency Medical
7\. Internet Connectivity

#### Good Light and Magnetism​

If you are looking for HARDCORE emf reduction, Atami Beach is the place to go. Though it is rather inconvenient to access the beach from wherever you might stay. If you are willing to trade a little more emf exposure for convenient beach access go with San Blas. If I remember correctly any place away from San Salvador and the airport are sufficient for getting better (watch out for cell towers of course) but the beach is ideal because you don't have to chase the sun and the volcanic sand has good magnetism.

#### Healthy Food​

There are regenerative / organic food options in El Salvador but expect to pay a hefty premium. There is a small chain of health food stores called Soya that I would recommend. The one by San Blas hosts a farmer's market regularly. Also, check out the Bitcoin Farmer's Market.

#### Language Barrier​

Once you leave the airport, there aren't many people who speak English. You will want to learn how to use Google Translate or a similar app to communicate. The locals don't seem to mind. Also, expect to have prices raised on you for being a foreigner.

#### Transportation​

Renting a car was absolutely NOT worth it. If you have never driven in a 3rd world country just use Uber. They are dirt cheap in ES and way less of a headache. So you have an idea: it cost me $27 to go an hour from the airport to San Blas. You could use the buses but I would recommend against it. If the drivers are in a hurry, they will start driving before you fully get off the bus which can be dangerous.

#### Emergency Medical​

You definitely want to know where the nearest emergency room while your there. I wasn't able to find any on the coast. The public emergency rooms are of questionable quality so I would suggest the private ones. Expect to pay up front and in cash. And remember that not all of them welcome foreigners. I used these two lists to locate a good emergency room for me: [List 1](https://sv.usembassy.gov/services/medical-assistance/), [List 2](https://www.gov.uk/government/publications/list-of-medical-facilities-in-el-salvador).

#### Internet Connectivity​

If you buy an international package for your current carrier it usually runs relatively expensive ($40/wk). I used Jetpac and got the $30 plan for one month of coverage. Easy peasy set up if you have a recent phone that supports eSIM.

* * *

That's all!


══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Hi Anna, If you put Swiss Shields into your curtains, what are you doing for the rest of the walls between you and your neighbors?
IF your bedroom is on the ground floor it may be more effective (and much less expensive) to put metal mesh up on the fence between you and them (if there is one). Metal mosquito net is cheep, easy to put up, can’t be seen and will block 90%+ of the RF coming from them to you. Think screen door on a microwave oven. Available from HomeDepot and/or Lowes. Alternatively you could put it on the outside of your house. You won’t block/stop Schumann which is a L-O-N-G wave.

Aluminum does not rust. Any hardware store will stock aluminum mosquito/window mesh.
If your fence is 4ft high but a 4ft wide roll. If 6ft buy a longer 3ft roll.
There is no RF from their panels. The RF is from their WiFi and will be blocked (90% reduced) by the wire mesh.
The solar panels are not a problem to you. Their inverter will be putting “DE” on the grid and affecting you - different issue.
A whole house “DE” filter will fix that.

# Thread: Catechol groups in acacia wood and the ark of the covenant
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/catechol-groups-in-acacia-wood-and-the-ark-of-the-covenant.32301/>
**Subforum:** The Cave

### Anthony Smith — 2026-02-26T00:01:07+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/catechol-groups-in-acacia-wood-and-the-ark-of-the-covenant.32301/post-367639>

> [Anthony Smith said:](/goto/post?id=367601)
>
> There are many building from antiquity, the Great Pyramid is just one, that would appear to be energy devices.
> Interesting note the “box” in the King’s chamber of the Great Pyramid is the same size as the Ark of the Covenant.

Well this is a lesson in not believing everything you read . . . Even on the Forum . . . Always double check before repeating.

I wrote the above about the Ark of the covenant and Great Pyramid sarcophagus being the same size from memory of multiple writings over the years. Many “famous” writers have made this claim. Turns out it is NOT true, “Similar“ but not the same.

The granite coffer in the Great Pyramid has interior measurements of 77.83 in. (1977 mm) in length by 26.65 in. (677 mm) in width, and 34.33 in (872 mm) in depth. The Ark of the Covenant is a bit harder to pin down since its measurements are less exact: “Have them make an ark of acacia wood—two and a half cubits long, a cubit and a half wide, and a cubit and a half high” (Exodus 25:10). The exact size of a cubit is disputable, but most scholars claim the size of the Ark at 45 inches in length by 27 inches in width and height on the standard conversion of 1 cubit to 18 imperial inches. However, another cubit, the so-called long cubit of approximately 20 inches, also existed, which would make the measurements 50 inches by 30 inches by 30 inches. However, the exact length of a cubit, to the millimeter, is unknown, so we just can’t be more exact—let alone make a model of “remarkable precision.”

So with that cleared up, it does not alter the fact that they are both VERY interesting and potentially ancient energy devices.

# Thread: Moral Dilemma
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/moral-dilemma.32321/>
**Subforum:** The Cave
**Posts:** 7
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Mr.AJ — 2026-02-27T19:55:47+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/moral-dilemma.32321/post-367755>

**Story time:**

There's an old guy who hangs out at a restaurant/social club in town. You have to have a membership get into the building every day, then you can hang out, have snacks, drinks, etc. He shows up a few times per week and just knocks on the window and waits for someone to let him in. I have never once seen him swipe himself in. Occasionally he will mumble about "I forgot my key at home" or something. While at the club he is very often the life of the party, chatty with everyone, constantly telling jokes and having a good time. He's fun and enjoys being there and from what I've seen has never been trouble with anyone. Some members do seem to have a problem with him, referring to him as a "dirty bum" on occasion, likely because he does not pay for a membership, and based on his general demeanor, it's not an unfair observation. But from what I've seen he's not a bad person.

**Scenario:**

Would buying him a membership be a morally good or bad thing to do for him? Money aside. I can think of many reasons for and against such as:

**For:**

\-An act of charity
\-He does not cause problems in general
\-Socialization is a healthy thing for him and this may be his primary outlet
\-It would reduce negativity from the members who do not like him "sneaking in"

**Against:**

\-He is a grown man who should be able to pay for his recreational activities
\-Based on our interactions, he seems like he might be the type to get a kick out of "sticking it to the man" or slipping one by the system (If he is immoral is he deserving or charity?). Meaning he may have the means to purchase a membership, he just doesn't because he is successfully sneaking in.
\-He gains no incentive to pay for his own membership once this one expires (broken enforcement system is the root problem here)
\-Helping people who do not help themselves is just enabling bad behavior.

I'm pretty sure if only the moral are deserving or charity, 99% of the population, myself included, is undeserving or charity. "He who is without sin cast the first stone, etc" Also Luke 6:38 and other verses basically encourage charity without judgement.

What do you think?

**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/moral-dilemma.32321/post-367757>

trust your gut feeling go with that

# Thread: New reason to shield all Wi-Fi
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-reason-to-shield-all-wi-fi.32346/>
**Subforum:** The Cave
**Posts:** 46
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Justin Goldberg — 2026-03-05T05:08:07+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/new-reason-to-shield-all-wi-fi.32346/post-368147>

I remember hearing about this on the EMF warriors podcast with smart meters.

Someone just turned your WiFi router into a full-body surveillance system.

No cameras. No wearables. No video. Just radio waves.

It's called RuView. It uses the WiFi signals already in your room to detect human poses, track breathing, measure heart rate, and see through walls.

Not a concept. Not a research paper. Working code you can run right now.

Here's what this thing actually does:

→ Tracks full 17-point body pose using only WiFi signals
→ Detects breathing rate (6-30 BPM) without touching anyone
→ Measures heart rate (40-120 BPM) from across the room
→ Sees through walls, furniture, and debris up to 5 meters deep
→ Tracks multiple people simultaneously with zero identity swaps
→ Self-learns from raw WiFi data. No labeled datasets needed

Here's how it works:

WiFi signals pass through your room and hit the human body. The body scatters those signals differently based on position, breathing, even heartbeat. RuView reads that scattering pattern and reconstructs everything.

A mesh of 4 ESP32 nodes ($48 total) gives you 360-degree coverage with 12 measurement links, 20 Hz updates, and sub-30mm precision.

Here's the wildest part:

It has a disaster response mode called WiFi-Mat. It detects survivors trapped under rubble through concrete walls, classifies injury severity using START triage protocol, and estimates 3D position. The kind of tool that saves lives after earthquakes.

The Rust implementation processes 54,000 frames per second. That's 810x faster than the Python version. The entire Docker image is 132 MB.

The AI model fits in 55 KB of memory. Runs on an $8 ESP32 chip.

Train once, deploy in any room. No retraining. No recalibration.

1,100+ tests. SHA-256 verified capability audit.

22.4K GitHub stars. 2.7K forks. MIT License.

100% Open Source.

### [GitHub - ruvnet/RuView: π RuView: WiFi DensePose turns commodity WiFi signals into real-time human pose estimation, vital sign monitoring, and presence detection — all without a single pixel of video.](https://github.com/ruvnet/RuView)

π RuView: WiFi DensePose turns commodity WiFi signals into real-time human pose estimation, vital sign monitoring, and presence detection — all without a single pixel of video. - ruvnet/RuView

 github.com

My hypothesis (with common example) in summary -

Radiofrequency (RF) fields - such as those emitted by devices like Wi-Fi routers, smart meters, or mobile phones - generate not only electromagnetic radiation but also structured informational fields. These arise from time-varying vector potentials and spin-based angular momentum topologies embedded within the EM wave itself. Even when the power density approaches zero (e.g., in distant exposure, shielded environments, or passive antenna systems), the vector potential component remains non-zero and can propagate long-range, phase-coherent effects. These informational fields interact with highly coherent biological structures, inducing quantum phase shifts, spin decoherence, and mitochondrial instability in ways completely independent of classical energy transfer.

The biological vulnerability to these effects is inversely related to systemic entropy. Coherent systems (i.e., high redox, low entropy) are more phase-sensitive and therefore more susceptible to subtle vector/torsion-based interference, while incoherent systems (low redox) are buffered by disorder but accumulate silent dysfunction. Electrohypersensitive (EHS) individuals represent the extreme of this coherence and thus act as biological sensors for invisible quantum-level disruption.

Should I keep going with this??"_

> If I can help them reduce their nnEMF exposure by 70% +/- TODAY - until they can move, that is not being a scammer - it is being PART of the solution.
>
> Helping people be informed and offering practical doable solutions also empowers them to choose a better place to live. ES (and Panama etc) have some crappy environments also.

I agree.

The other point I was trying to reconcile here is that in taking away the discomfort, we also take away the incentive to change, leading to complacency that turns the temporary 1st step into a permanent solution. The guilt of having helped someone into going down the wrong path is one that eats at you.

As long as we made it clear that what is offered is step 1 but the other person chooses to stop at that step, then the cross is for them and not for us to bear.

This is my first post - been following Jack since August 2024. My then 26 yo daughter at that time was walking with 2 canes from psoriatic arthritis. I still believe had we not found Jack, she would have been in a wheelchair within 6 months. She was deteriorating, fast. She was in her last year of college and was in a program that she could not take a break from or else she would have to start the program over. Mackenzie started implenting sunrise a few weeks after I found Jack and then she slowly started letting her feet ground and see the sun. She improved within a week and increased her time doing the strategies. Within 6 weeks, she had ditched the canes! We had a consult with Jack in mid Sept 2024 and by Dec 11, 2 days after Mackenzie's college break started, we were on a plane to El Salvador for 28 days. I was scared. She was not. I always went back to what I knew to be true and that calmed me. The things I knew to be true were the research I had done on the things Jack talked about, primarily El Salvador. Although Jack sounded angry (after all, it was an election year), I already understood what fueled his anger (the medical system and politics). I trusted him when he said El Sal was safe. We stayed in Shalpa with India and did the beach protocol from day 1. Within 24 hours, someone we were staying with said "Mackenzie, I do believe you are walking better already". We both agreed. It has been uphill ever since! I have a lot more I could add but I wanted to just hop on here and tell this little gem of a story in case you too were on the fence or worried about El Salvador or in disbelief about the sun etc. We have gone to El Salvador 3 times since that consult and have had nothing but great experiences there. I decided to write this today as I listened to Mackenzie walk upstairs on the floor above me - and I cannot tell which foot she is striking the floor with - which means her gait is near even! NO CANES! She is not out of the woods and still has a very long ways to go to truly reverse her condition, but she is working towards getting to El Salvador on a permanent basis and hoping to start that time there within a few months from now. Our environment in Kansas is not good. We both now know this and fully understand. I am working on being able to be there for sure during Kansas winters, longer if possible. We do the protocols at home as much as possible. The sun is the best medicine we have ever taken. : ) Thank you, Jack. On another post some time I will write about my journey .... and the punch in the mouth Jack gave me and what it did for me. Forever grateful.

Just to be extra clear on this based on the TF2 specs - anything below 0.1 could show zero.. So in your case of 0.0 to 0.1 oscillations the true field could be anywhere between the two as the meter cannot tell the difference as the flicker or oscillation could just represent quantisation + threshold crossing..

In the case of steady readings the + or - 4% accuracy would apply.. E.g. say you have 0.2mG true value could be ~ 0.192 - 0.208 mG..
This is EMF 101 basics say you have a smooth ramp from 0.1 - 0.2 as you walk in a direction this would identify the real gradient towards the source and may raise higher as you approach..

Just remember if you are serious about low levels it is important to have the necessary equipment with the required resolution, sensitivity and accuracy to measure it..

Think about a ruler - resolution = size of the markings vs accuracy of how well the ruler is calibrated etc.. You may be trying to measure 0.02mm with a ruler marked in 1mm increments.. Or for people in US still using the real system  say you have a ruler only in inch increments and trying to measure say 1.39" & your ruler can only show 1 or 2".. You get the picture?

Most of the values would get grouped into say discrete buckets or bins.. Bin 1 could be 0.00 - 0.049mG displays as 0.0 , Bin 2 could be 0.05 - 0.149 displays as 0.1mG and so on... It will round up and down..

If you use say a gigahertz solutions or equivalent with the necessary resolution - you may see a steady 0.02mG with out flicker... Hence the importance of having the correct equipment if you want an absolute on this (i.e. a real weak field or the meter operating at the resolution limit)...

# Thread: I made a food ranking excel
**Thread URL:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/i-made-a-food-ranking-excel.32460/>
**Subforum:** The Epi-Paleo Diet
**Posts:** 4
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
### Guy Houri — 2026-03-27T05:06:02+0200
**Source:** <https://forum.jackkruse.com/threads/i-made-a-food-ranking-excel.32460/post-369733>

### [food-tier](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1aq-eJu19cIsI8ChXzB_J33fKKI0O5kZCWZHJL3Y9qlo/edit?usp=sharing)

 docs.google.com

This Excel is not perfect but has helped me so maybe can give others inspiration / positive impact.
I went to the supermakret and categorized most of the things I saw.
I also might be wrong on some stuff there - I'll be happy to change it.

Every few months I updated my diet.
Standard American diet -> increasing protein (and plant proteins..) -> Intermittent fasting -> Increasing farmed meat -> half carnivore but not enough fat -> salmon everyday but farmed and not fatty -> Better meat, higher fat, some sardines

The final upgrade for now is heavily Seafood focused (still improvements to make) and lower carbs.
I have read the leptin, brain gut blogs, and searched the forum to see Jack's opinion on a lot of foods. Went to the supermarket and searched on everything I saw. Cost per KG, compared O3 amounts, is it farmed, is it in my latitude, is there more pesticide risk to this vegetable?
After creating this excel I was able to take the ingredients from the upper tiers, taste test which meals work for me, lower costs, and build a meal plan which reliefs me greatly.

The new kruse pyramid goes as:
Seafood (High DHA -> Colder water -> Wild -> Raw)
Meat (Organs -> Lamb -> Cattle -> Duck) & Eggs
Milk (Raw,A2) If pasturized still good for protein / farmed eggs / chicken
Vegetables (Seasonal, in latitude, low anti nutrients, low peticide risk, not coocked)
Seasonal fruits
Nuts & Seeds (Local, O3/O6)
Than the less optimal's also ranked

Tbh this took me weeks haha. Experimenting, analyzing, reading, building the Excel, and it is not done.
I have struggled in times with being "lost in the sauce", being in paralysis analysis of everything is toxic. And because of going out / eating one thing out of diet caused me a setback of days/weeks to getting back on track. I felt "I've already made poor decisions - might as well". This isn't completely in the past as well. I won't ever be truly optimized, and I will still occasionally enjoy eating out something not as healthy - something that took me a while to understand. But i'll do my best as to my knowledge. ranking food in an excel has quite helped me in all of this mess: see with my eyes what is better, handle budget, and upgrade my meal plan.

Hope this helps someone, if not, it helped me

Few notes:
\* In Israel there are many Russian people (Immigrated after USSR broke in 91) and there I found the cheapest canned fish and frozen fish. I tried getting boxes directly from suppliers but failed.
\* Iherb also has canned fish but a bit more expensive. Sometimes I prefer eating canned mussels which are a bit more expensive but are no work and tasty for me and make me full. Here is a link: [https://il.iherb.com/ugc/wishlist/share?id=4ec25a57-9275-4946-98bf-b9c7b0003130](https://il.iherb.com/ugc/wishlist/share?id=4ec25a57-9275-4946-98bf-b9c7b0003130)
\* the link for the excel is in the first comment but I also uploaded the excel as PDF here
